<script>
  (function ( o,$ ) {
    if( !o || !$ ) return false;

    var $o = $(o),
    clase = false,
    claseTlfn = false,
    idiomas = { 
      inp : o.querySelector('.sta-topHeader-eh_lang input'), 
      o : o.querySelector(".sta-topHeader-eh_lang"),
      remove : 0,
      list:null 
    },
    tlfns = {
      list : o.querySelector('.sta-topHeader-eh_tlfn ul').children,
      inp : o.querySelector('.sta-topHeader-eh_tlfn input')
    },
    control = function () {
      if( idiomas.inp.checked ){
        idiomas.inp.checked = false;
        $(idiomas.inp).change();
      }
      if( tlfns.list.length > 1 && tlfns.inp.checked ){
        tlfns.inp.checked = false;
        $(tlfns.inp).change();
      }
    };
    
    idiomas.lis = idiomas.o.querySelectorAll('ul li');

    for (var i = 0; i < idiomas.lis.length; i++) {
      (function( $li ){
        var url = $('a',$li).attr('href');
        if( !url || url.split('/').slice(-1).pop() == 'index.php' ){
          $li.remove();
          idiomas.remove++;
        }
      })( $(idiomas.lis[i]) );
    };

    if( idiomas.lis.length == idiomas.remove ) $(idiomas.o).addClass('sta-notIdiomas');

    $( o.querySelector(".sta-reservButton") ).click(function () {
      if ( window.openReservasGeneric ) openReservasGeneric();
    });

    $( o.querySelector(".sta-LoginButton") ).click(function () {
      if( window.modalLogin ) modalLogin();
    });

    $( document ).click( control );

    $(o).click(function(e){
      e.stopPropagation();
    });

    $(idiomas.inp).change(function(){
      if( this.checked && !clase ){
        clase = true;
        $o.addClass('sta-idiomasOpen');
      } else if( !this.checked && clase ){
        clase = false;
        $o.removeClass('sta-idiomasOpen');
      };
    });
    if( tlfns.list.length > 1 ){
      $(tlfns.inp).change(function(){
        if( this.checked && !claseTlfn ){
          claseTlfn = true;
          $o.addClass('sta-tlfnOpen');
        } else if( !this.checked && claseTlfn ){
          setTimeout(function(){
            claseTlfn = false;
            $o.removeClass('sta-tlfnOpen');
          },1000);
        };
      })
    }
    
  })( document.querySelector(".tpl-topHeader-eh"), window.jQuery );
</script>
